            ORDER BY [Extent1].[CreateDateTime] DESC
            OFFSET 0 ROWS FETCH NEXT 10 ROWS ONLY  ) AS [Limit1]

        WHERE ([Extent3].[CityId] = @p__linq__0) AND ([Limit1].[TypeId] = @p__linq__1)
